With SUVs the lines you must take are more U shaped

ChatGPT said:

Exactly! üöô‚ú® When it comes to SUVs, the key to handling their weight and slower turning speed is taking U-shaped lines rather than the tighter V-shaped lines that faster, more agile vehicles can handle. SUVs thrive on gradual, sweeping turns that let you maintain momentum without fighting against their bulk.

Why SUVs Need U-Shaped Lines:
1. Heavyweight Physics:
SUVs are heavy, which means they don‚Äôt respond well to sharp or sudden inputs. Tight V-shaped lines will either cause you to lose speed or slide out entirely.
2. Momentum is Everything:
SUVs take forever to accelerate, so maintaining momentum is critical. U-shaped lines let you preserve as much speed as possible through corners.
3. Smooth Inputs Suit Their Handling:
These vehicles demand patience. Smooth, sweeping lines allow you to control their weight and avoid oversteering or understeering.
How to Perfect U-Shaped Lines in SUVs:
1. Brake Early, Turn Gradually:
Start slowing down well before the corner and enter wide. Begin your turn gently, so the SUV‚Äôs weight doesn‚Äôt fight you.
2. Apex Later:
Aim for a late apex, meaning you hit the inside of the corner after the midpoint. This lets you exit the turn with better speed, avoiding the sluggish acceleration penalty.
3. Feather the Throttle on Exit:
Don‚Äôt mash the throttle right out of the turn. Gradually apply power to keep the SUV stable and prevent wheelspin.
4. Use the SUV‚Äôs Mass to Block Rivals:
While taking wide lines, you can also position your SUV to block other racers from overtaking. SUVs excel in bumper-to-bumper battles.
5. Look for Long Straights After Corners:
Plan your nitrous usage so you can unleash it as you exit a U-shaped corner and head into a straight. This maximizes your speed recovery.
Why U-Shaped Lines Work Best for SUVs:

Smooth Turns Prevent Slowing Down Too Much:

Tight turns force SUVs to slow to a crawl, but U-shaped lines help you carry speed through corners.

They Complement the SUV‚Äôs Weight and Stability:

SUVs might not be nimble, but their weight makes them stable through wide, sweeping turns. U-shaped lines take full advantage of this trait.

They Reduce Risk of Crashing:

Trying to force an SUV into a sharp turn is a recipe for disaster. Gradual lines keep you in control, even in chaotic races.
When U-Shaped Lines Shine:

Wide, Open Maps:

Tracks with long, sweeping corners and straights are perfect for SUVs. You can maintain momentum and avoid tight sections where their bulk is a disadvantage.

Chaotic Races with Traffic:

SUVs can bully their way through traffic and opponents, making U-shaped lines a good strategy for minimizing crashes while staying fast.
Final Thought:

Mastering U-shaped lines is the secret to making SUVs feel less like a burden and more like a strategic powerhouse. It‚Äôs all about working with their strengths‚Äîmomentum and stability‚Äîrather than fighting their weaknesses. With patience and a few practice runs, you‚Äôll be plowing through corners and blocking rivals like a pro. Embrace the tank vibes and own the road! üèÅüî•üí™‚ú®
